ReFrame logs

1. ReFrame scheduler script

#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name="rfm_RegressionTest_e5649a28"
#SBATCH --ntasks=1280
#SBATCH --ntasks-per-node=128
#SBATCH --cpus-per-task=1
#SBATCH --output=rfm_job.out
#SBATCH --error=rfm_job.err
#SBATCH --exclusive
#SBATCH --partition=qcpu
#SBATCH --account=dd-24-58
#SBATCH --threads-per-core=1
#SBATCH --time=0-00:15:0
module load OpenMPI/4.1.4-GCC-12.2.0
module load apptainer
srun --cpus-per-task=1 singularity exec -B"/scratch/project/dd-24-58/actions-runner/_work/bench.ktirio.fr/bench.ktirio.fr/build/reframe/stage/karolina/qcpu/default/RegressionTest_e5649a28:/rfm_workdir" --home /scratch/project/dd-24-58/apptainer_home --bind /scratch/project/dd-24-58/inputdataset:/input_data --env OMP_NUM_THREADS=1 /scratch/project/dd-24-58/images_sif/kub_feature-cem_partitioning-sif feelpp_kub_cem --config-files /input_data/kub/idealHeaters.cfg --cem.simulator.sun.filename=/input_data/kub/simulators/Sun.fmu --cem.simulator.lod0.modelisation.maxfloors=10 --cem.preprocessing.dataregistry.directory=/input_data/kub_benchmark/Paris/3km/preprocessing --cem.weather.filename=/input_data/kub/Paris/weather.csv --cem.scenarios.filename=/input_data/kub/scenarios_local/scenarios.json --cem.instance.time.start=0 --cem.instance.time.stop=86400 --cem.instance.time.step=3600 --cem.instance.postprocess.export.visualization.enabled=false --cem.instance.postprocess.export.report.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.csv.enabled=false --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.enabled=false --cem.instance.solar_shading.enabled=true --cem.instance.idealflows.enabled=true --cem.database.directory /scratch/project/dd-24-58/apptainer_home/kub/e5649a28/SM_Quadrature_Order --directory /scratch/project/dd-24-58/apptainer_home/kub/e5649a28/SM_Quadrature_Order --cem.instance.solar_shading.ray-tracing.quad-order 0

     - Likely caused by over-using noEvent.
  Especially consider the first two items above when the nonlinear solver fails during initialization.

  To get more information consider the options:
   * Simulation/Setup/Translation/Generate listing of translated Modelica code in dsmodel.mof
   * Simulation/Setup/Translation/List non-linear iteration variables
   * Simulation/Setup/Debug/Store variables after failed initialization
     - If a failure to solve a nonlinear equation caused failed initialization.
   * The options under the group Simulation/Setup/Debug/Nonlinear solver diagnostics
